Gibson
3 1/2 oz. Gin
1/2 oz. Vermouth (Dry)
Garnish: Cocktail Onions
Pour vodka or gin and the vermouth into a shaker with ice. Stir to chill the contents. Strain into a chilled martini glass.CommentsDry means less vermouth. Extra Dry means a lot less vermouth. The only difference between a Martini and a Gibson is the garnish. Martini comes with olives or a lemon twist while a Gibson comes with cocktail onions.

Tequila Shot
2 oz. Tequila (Premium)
Garnish: Lime Wedge and Salt
Moist the rim of a shot glass with a lime and dip it into kosher salt. Pour the premium tequila into the shot glass. Lick the salt, take the shot and bite the lime.CommentsIf you rather use the orange slice, don't use salt. Just take the shot of tequila and bite the orange slice. Do not use the lime and the orange together. I like the orange better.

Agua De Tamarindo
10 oz. Dried Tamarinds (Peeled)
10 Cups of Water
1 Cup of Sugar
Garnish: No Garnish
Wash the tamarinds and soak them in 4 cups of hot water for a couple of hours. Rub the tamarinds against each other to get as much pulp as possible. Strain the mixture into a pitcher and dilute with 6 cups of cold water. Add sugar to taste.CommentsEnglish Name: Tamarind Water

Agua De Horchata
2 Cups of Long-Grain White Rice
7 Cups of Water
2 Cups of Milk
2 Cinnamon Sticks
1 Cup of Sugar
Garnish: No Garnish
Soak rice in 3 cups of water for a couple of hours. Crumble cinnamon and toast it on a small skillet. Strain the rice and blend it with the cinnamon and milk. Strain mixture into a pitcher and dilute it with 4 cups of water. Add sugar to taste.CommentsEnglish Name: Ground Rice Drink

Agua De Jamaica
2 Cups of Dried Hibiscus
10 Cups of Water
1 Cup of Sugar
Garnish: No Garnish
Place Hibiscus flowers in a pan with 6 cups of water. Bring to boil for a couple of minutes. Remove the pan from the heat and let it cool for 20 minutes. Strain the water into a pitcher and dilute it with 4 cups of cold water. Add sugar to taste.CommentsEnglish Name: Hibiscus Iced Tea

Pour all ingredients except the club soda into a shaker with ice. Shake and strain into a glass with ice. Fill it with club soda.

1 oz. Coffee Liqueur
1/2 oz. Maraschino Liqueur
1 oz. Cream / Half & Half
Garnish: No Garnish
Pour Scotch, coffee liqueur and maraschino liqueur into a shaker with ice. Shake and pour into an old-fashioned glass. Float the cream on top.
